<span id="freeTextContainer14583391117871692342">Pongo and Perdita are the proud parents of fifteen Dalmation puppies. When the evil Cruella de Vil steals Dalmation puppies from all over the countryside, their litter is taken as well. Pongo and Perdita enlist the help of other animals to track down and save the puppies only to find that their family has now grown to include 101 Dalmations.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_981127009">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/981127009" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/1757121-sharon" class="left imgcol" title="Sharon"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1293544980p2/1757121.jpg" alt="Sharon" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/981127009?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jun 29, 2014</a>

      <a href="/user/show/1757121-sharon" class="user" title="Sharon">Sharon</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/2322209.101_Dalmatians" title="Hardcover 9780736424202" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/1757121-sharon?shelf=young-at-heart" class="actionLinkLite">young-at-heart</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer981127009">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13128507713833199653">I attended a lecture on the art of Little Golden Books, and found this delightful version of a childhood favorite available for sale. It is, of course, a highly condensed version of Dodie Smith's <a title="The Hundred and One Dalmatians (The Hundred and One Dalmatians, #1) by Dodie Smith" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/511614.The_Hundred_and_One_Dalmatians__The_Hundred_and_One_Dalmatians___1_">The Hundred and One Dalmatians</a>, with delightful illustrations reminiscent of the beloved Disney movie.<br /><br />We see Pongo and Perdita, with the help of their animal friends, rescue not just their own puppies but many, many more from the clutches of Cruella deVil and her henchmen.<br /><br />Sweet little book.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_502062519">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/502062519" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/12710027-tyler-steinback" class="left imgcol" title="Tyler Steinback"><img src="http://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" alt="Tyler Steinback" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/502062519?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jan 11, 2013</a>

      <a href="/user/show/12710027-tyler-steinback" class="user" title="Tyler Steinback">Tyler Steinback</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/2322209.101_Dalmatians" title="Hardcover 9780736424202" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer502062519">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1253995256727175367">In the story "101 Dalmatians" Cruella De Vil went to Roger and Anita's house to buy their little puppies. Roger and Anita didn't want to sell them. Cruella De Vil got very angry, and hired two men to steal the puppies. I liked this book because Pongo and Perdita didn't give up when their puppies were stolen. I would recommend this book to kids that are learning to read, because it is an easy read and a fun story. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_451735306">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/451735306" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/1798996-valerie" class="left imgcol" title="Valerie"><img src="http://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" alt="Valerie" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/451735306?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Nov 08, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/1798996-valerie" class="user" title="Valerie">Valerie</a>

          added it


          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/1298154.101_Dalmatians" title="Hardcover " class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer451735306">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17203205760379799792">Speaking of Disney novelizations (as some of us were earlier), this is one of the novelizations I read before I saw the movie it came from. <br /><br />I have to say I preferred the book version. The movie was fun, but it struck me as sort of...I search for a word. Flighty, maybe? Too much action, and too little exposition, I mean. I liked the exposition in the book version.<br /><br />Too many recent movies strike me as resembling thunderstorms: light flashes, clashes of thunder, sudden changes of scene, raucous music</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17203205760379799792">Speaking of Disney novelizations (as some of us were earlier), this is one of the novelizations I read before I saw the movie it came from. <br /><br />I have to say I preferred the book version. The movie was fun, but it struck me as sort of...I search for a word. Flighty, maybe? Too much action, and too little exposition, I mean. I liked the exposition in the book version.<br /><br />Too many recent movies strike me as resembling thunderstorms: light flashes, clashes of thunder, sudden changes of scene, raucous music, and too many chase scenes. I can enjoy such things only so far--then it starts getting really trying. <br /><br />Among Disney properties, I regard this as pretty much the precursor of that sort of thing. Having a chance to sit down and catch my breath between action scenes in the book was a real plus, as I remember it.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="17203205760379799792">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vBGAxaRGMZWK+fgB4F1WknjKJhwEVouxYTq2abo1wW/Zxb8WVpQlbwYhjLqePLAgMT3lBU2LzBsLM7P7dqA3Kg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OBp/ydvFsl40hBjiSWGqXRZ5eyMGpsOPkLrgcqa3ttldzkAaKRempLhcbFk3AEzvX464Ok97hCX6s+XgaiJAnA==')})
  }

And there begin the fantastical adventures that will see her experiencing extraordinary changes in size, swimming in a pool of her own tears and attending the very maddest of tea parties. For Wonderland is no ordinary place and the characters that populate it are quite unlike anybody young Alice has ever met before. In this imaginary land she encounters the savagely violent Queen, the Lachrymose Mock Turtle, the laconic Cheshire Cat and the hookah-smoking Caterpillar, each as surprising and outlandish as the next. Alice\'s adventures have made her the stuff of legend, the child heroine par excellence, and ensured that Carroll\'s book is the best loved and most widely read in children\'s literature.Charles Lutwidge Dodgson, celebrated under his pseudonym Lewis Carroll, was born in 1832, the third in a large and talented family of eleven children. His fascination with word games, puzzles and writing was evident from an early age. He was educated at Rugby School and then Christ Church, Oxford, where he was later appointed lecturer in mathematics and subsequently spent the rest of his life. Alongside his academic life he pursued a career both as a writer and an accomplished amateur photographer. His most famous works are Alice\'s Adventures in Wonderland (1865), its sequel Through the Looking Glass and What Alice Found There (1871) and The Hunting of the Snark (1876). He died, unmarried, in 1898.The handsome volumes in The Collectors Library present great works of world literature in a handy hardback format. Printed on high-quality paper and bound in real cloth, each complete and unabridged volume has a specially commissioned afterword, brief biography of the author and a further-reading list. This easily accessible series offers readers the perfect opportunity to discover, or rediscover, some of the world\'s most endearing literary works.The volumes in The Collector\'s Library are     <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/303859.Justine_Korman_Fontes">About Justine Korman Fontes</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/303859.Justine_Korman_Fontes"><img alt="303859" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1309470678p2/303859.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer3727102443821375823">Justine Korman is the author of over 600 children's books, including mega-selling adaptations of Disney hits like THE LION KING, plus her original popular GRUMPY BUNNY series for Scholastic.<br /><br />Justine has been writing all her life. She worked part-time in publishing while earning her B.A. in English Literature, Phi Beta Kappa from New York University. While an editorial assistant at Golden Books, she</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText3727102443821375823">Justine Korman is the author of over 600 children's books, including mega-selling adaptations of Disney hits like THE LION KING, plus her original popular GRUMPY BUNNY series for Scholastic.<br /><br />Justine has been writing all her life. She worked part-time in publishing while earning her B.A. in English Literature, Phi Beta Kappa from New York University. While an editorial assistant at Golden Books, she met her future husband and partner, Ron Fontes, an artist in the Whitman Comics department, who moved on to mighty Marvel Comics.<br /><br />When Justine started getting freelance writing assignments, Ron pitched in and a children's book writing team was born! Ron brought visual storytelling, theatre, and history; Justine enthusiasm, humor, and a straight-A attitude.<br /><br />In 1988, the couple moved to Maine, where they have written everything from beginning readers and novelty books to historical fiction and graphic novels.<br />Justine's hobbies include fitness, juggling, gardening, cooking, and playing the ukulele. She also enjoys making movies with Ron.<br /><br />The prolific couple's goal is to write 1001 children's books.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="3727102443821375823">...more</a>

    </div>
